#### The substitution functor of group actions

<pre class="Agda"><a id="28023" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="28030" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28030" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="28034" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28035" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28035" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="28038" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28038" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="28041" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28043" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="28048" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28050" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28051" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28051" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="28053" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28055" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#23569" class="Function">Group</a> <a id="28061" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28035" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="28063" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28065" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28066" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28066" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="28068" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28070" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#23569" class="Function">Group</a> <a id="28076" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28038" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="28078" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28080" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28081" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28081" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28083" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28085" href="groups.abstract-groups.html#29850" class="Function">type-hom-Group</a> <a id="28100" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28051" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="28102" href="groups.abstract-group-actions.html#28066" class="Bound">H</a><a id="28103" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="28107" class="Keyword">where</a>

#### Orbits
